The function should have a time complexity of O(n), where n is the length of the input array, and a space complexity of O(1). <NL>  <NL> arr = [4, 2, 5, 1, 6] <NL>  <NL> Write your solution below: <NL>  <NL> def max_diff(arr): <NL>     if len(arr) < 2: <NL>         return None <NL>      <NL>     max_diff = arr[1] - arr[0] <NL>     min_element = arr[0] <NL>  <NL>     for i in range(1, len(arr)): <NL>         if arr[i] - min_element > max_diff: <NL>             max_diff = arr[i] - min_element <NL>          <NL>         if arr[i] < min_element: <NL>             min_element = arr[i] <NL>      <NL>     return max_diff <NL>  <NL> arr = [4, 2, 5, 1, 6] <NL> print(max_diff(arr)) # Output: 5 (6 - 1) <NL>  <NL> # Additional test cases <NL> arr_1 = [10, 9, 8, 7, 6]  <NL> print(max_diff(arr_1)) # Output: -1 (9 - 10) <NL>  <NL> arr_2 = [-3, -1, 4, 7, 12]  <NL> print(max_diff(arr_2)) # Output: 5 (12 - 7) <NL>  <NL> arr_3 = [5] <NL> print(max_diff(arr_3)) # Output: None (len < 2)  <NL>  <NL> arr_4 = [] <NL> print(max_diff(arr_4)) # Output: None (len < 2)\ <NL>  <NL> \subsection*{Closing Note} <NL> That concludes our task for today.
